if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != '24c6f42b6b6e64806904b66e6342e8c4de228696') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '24c6f42b6b6e64806904b66e6342e8c4de228696') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '9aa75d23e9038fcfac1ebf3210f47f671eab660d') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '24c6f42b6b6e64806904b66e6342e8c4de228696') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

}

if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/functions.inc.php');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('includes/functions.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') != '13f06f9434769b9f07765ccc82214e46690b00b7') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/functions.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/functions.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '13f06f9434769b9f07765ccc82214e46690b00b7') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== 'ac51d9360a467efc205af59d427aba70b834c0a7') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/functions.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/functions.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/functions.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/functions.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/functions.inc.php') !== '13f06f9434769b9f07765ccc82214e46690b00b7') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/functions.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

	if (!is_file('oidplus.min.js.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus.min.js.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus.min.js.php') != 'df713179f2657a20661b84eeeead8f7ceeaa0bdc') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus.min.js.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus.min.js.php', 0644)) {

	}

	if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.js.php') !== 'df713179f2657a20661b84eeeead8f7ceeaa0bdc') {

			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus.min.js.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');

			if (!@copy('oidplus.min.js.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.js.php') !== 'df713179f2657a20661b84eeeead8f7ceeaa0bdc') {

if (!is_file('setup/setup.min.js.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/setup.min.js.php');
	writefile_9();
	if (!is_file('setup/setup.min.js.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/setup.min.js.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/setup.min.js.php') != 'cd06cab783e2d1e151c033286d7531c5c51295cc') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/setup.min.js.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/setup.min.js.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/setup.min.js.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.min.js.php') !== 'cd06cab783e2d1e151c033286d7531c5c51295cc') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.min.js.php') !== 'a3aeb1be9906ecc9e8824ada2db85f3420807bc8') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/setup.min.js.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/setup.min.js.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/setup.min.js.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/setup.min.js.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_9();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.min.js.php') !== 'cd06cab783e2d1e151c033286d7531c5c51295cc') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/setup.min.js.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('update/index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: update/index.php');
	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('update/index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): update/index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('update/index.php') != 'a7b8467fd94b19e6ed34fc9cade39dac40aab632') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): update/index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('update/index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of update/index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== 'a7b8467fd94b19e6ed34fc9cade39dac40aab632') {
		if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== 'ee9832855ddc516cfa636d7168bbe87d2709fba3') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: update/index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('update/index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('update/index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('update/index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== 'a7b8467fd94b19e6ed34fc9cade39dac40aab632') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): update/index.php');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 486\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 486') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
